# Text Elements

Locations ^v1iVevWY

Yemen ^Zv13yPde

Ancient Marib Dam ^NYR6GSxl

Like previous civilizations, they disobeyed Allah and the dam was therefore destroyed, so the Arab tribes migrated to neighboring places  ^LZthZcp1

One of these tribes, called Jurhum, went to Mecca, where they found the well of zamzam ^Evewm664

[[Islamic Stories/Arabs/The History Of Arabs.excalidraw.md#^Evewm664|Banu Jurhum]] ^jokTAF1k

Banu Khuza'ah ^hGwrMnPw

They fought Banu Jurhum for the leadership of Mecca and won ^nKfdXFwl

As payback, Banu Jurhum covered the well of Zamzam, and it remained hidden for centuries ^p5PWGG5z

Allah later made a certain person dream about its whereabouts and uncover it. This person was Shaiba ibn HƒÅshim, also known as  øAbd al-Mu·π≠·π≠alib who was the grandfather of Prophet Muhammad (PBUH) ^eb3Qw0dg

Later, a respected leader of Mecca named Amr ibn Luhayy was appointed as head of the tribe in Mecca ^WiT8Eypa

He was a business man who used to travel between Mecca and Syria (called Ash-Sham back then), where it was common to go to Syria in summer and Yemen in winter to bring traded resources back to Mecca ^lNXeMhIN

So one day he travelled to Syria and met with the Amalek tribe, where they used to worship hand-crafted idols and take them as a connection to their Lord ^ajwR7QJ5

So Amr ibn Luhayy took one of the idols, called Hubal, back to Mecca, and ordered everyone to worship this idol, thus changing the Arab's religion from worshipping Allah to worshipping idols ^MTpoY68g

He then ordered for other idols to be manufactured for different purposes (moon, sun, food, etc.), and they were placed around the Kaaba ^TGe7A6ee

A Yemeni king by the name of [Rabia ibn Nasr](https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Rabiah_Ibn_Nasr) had a bad dream, and called for two magicians (i.e., soothsayer) to interpret that dream ^n2gpIchX

[Years later](https://www.facebook.com/ProphetMuhamadBiography/photos/chapter-onemecca-in-the-spotlighttranslated-by-roger-owens-muhammad-qutuzyemen-4/208512189574451/?paipv=0&eav=AfaKSOiSFPO7aAj91OqSp5AGzIzSeQKfJa1nFMNEE1qwXOrrFwqNzA_zac0lpuw-Lcs&_rdr) ^tRmhF1Mp

Mecca ^9vr57mWB

Both magicians said that there will come a time where a tribe of black people from Sudan or Ethiopia will come and take over Yemen ^wFV6AoHu

So, Rabia migrated with his family from Yemen to  [[https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Najran|Najran]], which was linked to Ash-Sham (currently the countries of Syria, Lebanon, Jordon, & Palestine) ruled by the Roman empire ^DvpWkKTq

Years later, he died and his son [[https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Abu_Karib#introduction|Abu Karib As'ad al-Kamil]] wanted to go back to Yemen ^yPFWPP2F

On his way to Yemen, he conquered Yathrib (currently called [[https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Medina|Medina]]) and made his son its governor. Later on he discovered that the people of Yathrib killed his son, so he halted his journey to Yemen, and went back to Yathrib to avenge his son ^dLy9TPPS

At that time, [[Islamic Stories/Arabs/The History Of Arabs.excalidraw.md#^MAKTVCHP|Yathrib had multiple Jewish tribes]]; Banu Qurayza, Qaynuqa, and Nadir ^9DU6jMiP

So by day, Abu Karib would would fight the people of Yathrib, and by night, they would offer him hospitality by giving him food ^x7PEQ3wi

This is because the people of Yathrib were (and still are) always showing hospitality and generosity to foreigners! ^ptGIrJu2

[[https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Banu_Qurayza|Banu Qurayza]] ^l8ZoVzwo

[[Islamic Stories/Arabs/The History Of Arabs.excalidraw.md#^9DU6jMiP|Jewish tribes in Yathrib]] ^MAKTVCHP

[[https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Banu_Qaynuqa|Banu Qaynuqa]] ^om2sGCXr

[[https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Banu_Nadir|Banu Nadir]] ^6wlPjGkB

Two Jewish scholars from Banu Qurayza came to Abu Karib, advised him not to invade Yathrib as it is protected by Allah because soon a üîó prophet will reach it, and gave him teachings day by day until he listened to their advice and converted to Judaism ^cv8VEQpx

He then went back with the two scholars to Yemen, and on the way there, he met two Arabs who wanted to plot against him and Quraysh, so they told him to destroy the Kaaba to obtain the jewelry beneath it ^TyGNLXTd

However, the two Jewish scholars advised him to perform pilgrim around it instead, as it is protected by Allah, so he killed the two Arabs who were trying to deceive him, and performed pilgrimage  ^dXotyC0q

Later on, Abu Karib (known as Tubban As'ad) [[The Kaaba|covered the Kaaba]] each time he had a dream of covering it the day before, and thus he became the first one to fully cover the Kaaba ^a7ZFjLOP

When he finally went to Yemen, the [[https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Himyarite_Kingdom|Himyar tribes]] refused to let him or his two scholars as he embraced Judaism instead of [[https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Idolatry|Idolism (ÿßŸÑŸàÿ´ŸÜŸäÿ©)]] ^3Ckf7VhJ

When there was a dispute over a religious matter, the Himyarites used to open the door of a house that contained a great fire and the two disputing parties would stand far from each other near that door, so whichever party gets destroyed by the fire is considered as the losing party ^EDwNfTrs

The fire then consumed the people of Himyar, so upon seeing this, the people of Yemen converted to Judaism ^ExGqPaxw

The fire then consumed the people of Himyar, so upon seeing this, the people of Yemen converted to Judaism ^NNGIrgiT

Tribes in Yemen ^jubiE8MG

[[Islamic Stories/Arabs/The History Of Arabs.excalidraw.md#^3Ckf7VhJ|Banu Himyar]] ^0B9OrMpR

Abu Kabir (i.e., As'ad) later had a son called Hassan who became the next king of Yemen, and who wanted to take over the Arab peninsula even if it costs great sufferings to the army of Yemen ^KkAUuP9h

Amr agreed, killed his brother, then because of his guilt went to some fortune tellers who told him to kill all the generals that deceived him in order to stop feeling guilty, so he killed them all except [[https://youtu.be/tEB4xdSkcX4?t=119|Dhƒ´ Ra øƒ´n (ÿ∞Ÿä ÿ±ÿπŸäŸÜ)]] ^epZp9eDe

Amr later died of depression, and a gangster Hymarite called [[https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Dhu_Shanatir|Dhu Shanatir (ŸÑÿÆŸÜŸäÿπÿ© ÿ∞Ÿä ÿ¥ŸÜÿßÿ™ÿ±)]] ruled Yemen until [[https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Dhu_Nuwas|Dhu Nuwas (ÿ∞ŸèŸà ŸÜŸèŸàŸéÿßÿ≥)]], brother of Amr and Hassan, stabbed him ^yyPkcSUk

Because of this, all army generals, except a Hymarite man called Dhƒ´ Ra øƒ´n (ÿ∞Ÿä ÿ±ÿπŸäŸÜ), plotted against him by deceiving his brother, Amr, to overthrow Hassan and become king instead ^ewzGNbI1

Now, magic was an important aspect for the Jews of Yemen, so when one of the main magicians of Dhu Nuwas was getting old, Dhu Nuwas decided to choose from his town a young child to learn from this old magician   ^togMdgNK

On his way to the magician, the child would pass by a tent where he heard the praying of a Christian scholar (who migrated to Yemen from Najran) ^jCibZydJ

As a side note, Najran became dominated by Christians when a Christian slave by the name of Fimyon asked Allah (SWT) to send a thunder upon a palm tree that was worshipped at that time ^TuQWPI9D

The child was interested to know more about this scholar, so each day, the child would be taught by him then by Dhu Nuwas's magician   ^qhIVZnUY

Allah then bestowed upon the child the gift of healing people, so when Dhu Nuwas asked him how he was more proficient in magic than his magician, the child told him that it wasn't because of magic, but because of Allah (SWT)  ^w2ucNHxm

Upon hearing this, Dhu Nuwas got very angry and ordered his soldiers to search for a Christian scholar who might have taught the child about Christianity  ^lWR0xm2i

They then brought the previously mentioned scholar to Dhu Nuwas, and he killed him, then he tried to force the child to follow Judaism instead, but the child refused ^tuojWy2Y

So he ordered his soldiers to drown the child in the middle of the sea, but they died on the way (due to the child's prayers to Allah) and then he returned to Dhu Nuwas, who ordered other soldiers to throw him from the peak of a mountain, in which they failed again for the same reason, then the child returned again ^oybQa8Vn

The child then said that the only way to kill him, is for Dhu Nuwas to tie him up in a tree, gather the people of Yemen around them, and get an arrow thrower to say "in the name of the Lord of this young man" and then shoot him. ^YPAdOd7R

so only when Dhu Nuwas did those things was he able to kill the child ^RuPOCRcE

When the people of Yemen saw that, 20000 of them followed Christianity instead of Judaism ^BvZTd6LM

So Dhu Nuwas and his soldiers dug up a ditch, filled it with fire, and threw anyone who refused to go back to Judaism    ^1afDmb5p

Only one man, called [[https://abdurrahman.org/2014/01/31/storyofboyandking/#:~:text=was%20known%20as-,Daws%20Dhu%20Tha%60laban,-.%20He%20escaped%20on|Daws Dhu Tha`laban (ÿ∞Ÿà ÿ´ÿπŸÑÿ®ÿßŸÜ)]], fled from Yemen to Caesar, the Roman emperor of Ash-Sham, who wrote to An-Najashi, the king of Abyssinia (Euthopia), who sent a Christian army of 70000 man to Yemen ^qVzcW8Tk

This army was lead by Aryat and Abraha, and was able to rescue Yemen from Dhu Nuwas (who tried to flee but drowned) ^s6NxiY21

Aryat was now leading Yemen, but because of his cruelty, Abraha killed him and became the leader instead, so when An-Najashi heard this, he made an oath to go to Yemen, cut the hair of Abrahah, and step on it ^R9l9lqZH

So when Abraha heard of this news, he sent a diplomatic letter to An-Najashi along with a bag of his shaved hair and sand of Yemen for An-Najashi to fulfill his oath by stepping on it instead of killing Abraha ^7t3VM5ME

So An-Najashi endorsed him, and Abraha wanted to maintain that endorsement by building a massive church in Yemen called [[https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Al-Qalis_Church,_Sanaa|Al-Qalis]], and by turning the people away from the Kaaba ^Yq5ISJwm

The Arab didn't like this news to the point that one of them dud his natural call in Al-Qalis church and spread his faeces around its walls ^pdmXjW9C

When Abraha knew about this, he went out with his great army to destroy the Kaaba, and would destroy every tribe that fights him ^PWQI2k3R

Along the way, he went to [[https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Taif|Taif]] where its tribe surrendered to him, and one of them by the name of [[https://www.wikiwand.com/ar/%D8%A3%D8%A8%D9%88_%D8%B1%D8%BA%D8%A7%D9%84|Abu Ru'al (ÿ£ÿ®Ÿà ÿ±ÿ∫ÿßŸÑ)]] guided him to the place of the Kaaba, but he died and got buried on the way there ^7xVJBsra

Later, Abraha found Mecca and camped on its borders, where he ordered his soldiers to take the life stock of the people of Mecca. From among those, 200 camels were taken that belong to [[https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Abd_al-Muttalib|Shaiba ibn Hashim (known as Abd al-Muttalib)]] ^tp3f7IBX

After collecting life stock, Abraha met the leader of Mecca, who was Abd al-Muttalib, and Abraha asked him what he wants. Abd al-Muttalib said he wanted his camels back, so Abraha was shocked and asked him how he did not think about his town and only mentioned his camels ^K8GFYGZk

So Abd al-Muttalib told Abraha that he is the lord (i.e., owner) of these camels, while this Kaaba, has a Lord that will look after it  ^BPT7sdRc

Upon hearing this, Abraha returned his camels, and Abd al-Muttalib went back to Mecca and told its people to temporarily leave Mecca and head to its surrounding mountains ^5LI511fb

Abraha then came with army and a huge elephant by the name of [[https://www.wikiwand.com/en/Year_of_the_Elephant|Mahmud]] to destroy the Kaaba, but whenever Mahmud was looking towards the Kaaba and getting near it, he would stop moving ^yZwgcLWy

They then saw a black cloud coming towards them and hundreds of birds with stones; one on its beaks and two in its claws. The birds then destroyed Abraha and his army with special stones, and that was a sign to all people that the Kaaba was a place protected by Allah (SWT) ^GRNve5Qx

After the destruction of Abraha and his army, Yemen, was led by his two sons, and was then led by the Persian empire (where the king was called [[Terminologies#^uodq5d|Kisra]]) during the time of the Prophet Muhammad ^1mausxOo
